                 <a class="no-u" data-pb-field="headlines.basic" data-pb-field-type="text" data-pb-placeholder="Write headline here" data-pb-url-field="canonical_url" data-tr-content-id="XN6A473XGNG4NESPW6AGXWD4KU" href="/business/careers-finance/sns-ways-you-unintentionally-commit-tax-fraud-20210316-xn6a473xgng4nespw6agxwd4ku-photogallery.html">
                  12 ways you may be accidentally committing tax fraud
                 </a>
                </p>
               </div>
               <div class="preview-text spaced spaced-top story-preview spaced-md hddn-mble hddn-dktp hddn-tbl hddn-mble" data-pb-field="description.basic" data-pb-field-type="text" data-pb-placeholder="Write blurb here.">
                While some errors on your tax returns are honest mistakes that can be corrected, your efforts to game the system or get more of a return may teeter on the edge of outright tax fraud. Check out this information from the IRS’s website and their 2019 “Dirty Dozen” list of the worst tax scams to find out some of the ways you may be accidentally committing tax fraud.
               </div>
               <div class="spaced spaced-sm spaced-top byline-container flex-container-row align-items-center">

                </div>

             <div class="crd--cnt align-items-start flex-container-row justify-space-between">
              <div class="art width-100 spaced spaced-right spaced-lg flex-2-col river">
               <figure class="cls-height" data-trk-photo-credit="">
                <div class="full-width img-container asp-rto-4x3-mb aspect-ratio-4x3">
                 <a href="/coronavirus/hc-viz-coronavirus-flu-epidemic-connecticut-courant-pages-20200414-vrldbr5zrjh6rj4ayyiejeeqva-photogallery.html" tabindex="-1">
                  <img alt="From closed schools to banned gatherings, Courant pages from 1918 show similarities between coronavirus and 1918 flu pandemic" class="b-lazy full-width1" data-src="https://www.courant.com/resizer/aB2IlNIj7nK56P0JUgN7v_RZq3E=/1200x900/top/cloudfront-us-east-1.images.arcpublishing.com/tronc/NVNOJ7RFCRHSFCR3VG3O3ITASU.png" data-src-medium="https://www.courant.com/resizer/vAa7Ayew8dfOkR4Li1lgDfZfm8I=/800x600/top/cloudfront-us-east-1.images.arcpublishing.com/tronc/NVNOJ7RFCRHSFCR3VG3O3ITASU.png" data-src-mobile="https://www.courant.com/resizer/1ttyguGM26EOFYT135fjxmeZmRQ=/415x311/top/cloudfront-us-east-1.images.arcpublishing.com/tronc/NVNOJ7RFCRHSFCR3VG3O3ITASU.png" data-src-small="https://www.courant.com/resizer/1ttyguGM26EOFYT135fjxmeZmRQ=/415x311/top/cloudfront-us-east-1.images.arcpublishing.com/tronc/NVNOJ7RFCRHSFCR3VG3O3ITASU.png" src="/pb/resources/images/tinygif.gif?v=274"/>
                 </a>
                 <ul class="tag-list-wrapper list-unstyled flex-container-row lead-story-topic" role="presentation">
                  <li class="li--topic--it">
                   <a class="tag tag-solid tag-first" href="https://www.courant.com/coronavirus/#nt=taxonomy-article">
                    Coronavirus
                   </a>
                  </li>
                 </ul>
                </div>
               </figure>
               <style>
                img.full-width1{flex-shrink:0;object-fit:contain;min-height:50%;height:auto;width:100%}
               </style>
              </div>
              <div class="width-100 flex-container-column flex river">
               <div class="">
                <p class="r-mb h6">
                 <a class="no-u" data-pb-field="headlines.basic" data-pb-field-type="text" data-pb-placeholder="Write headline here" data-pb-url-field="canonical_url" data-tr-content-id="VRLDBR5ZRJH6RJ4AYYIEJEEQVA" href="/coronavirus/hc-viz-coronavirus-flu-epidemic-connecticut-courant-pages-20200414-vrldbr5zrjh6rj4ayyiejeeqva-photogallery.html">
                  From closed schools to banned gatherings, Courant pages from 1918 show similarities between coronavirus and 1918 flu pandemic
                 </a>
                </p>
               </div>
               <div class="preview-text spaced spaced-top story-preview spaced-md" data-pb-field="description.basic" data-pb-field-type="text" data-pb-placeholder="Write blurb here.">
                Colleges canceled classes, bars were shut down, movies weren't released and public gatherings were banned. It sounds a lot like the 2020 coronavirus outbreak, but this was 1918 and the influenza pandemic was spreading across the country. A look back through the Courant's archives show some striking similarities between the responses to stop the spread.

                            ad.setAttribute('data-keyvalues', JSON.stringify(keyValues))

                            if(window.zeus) {
                              zeus.emit("RESET_KEYVALUES")
                            }
                          }
                          if((!DeviceDetection.isDesktopSize() && true) || (DeviceDetection.isDesktopSize() && true)) {
                            trb.zeus.addKVs(document.getElementById("zeus_cc_230"));
                          }
            </script>
           </div>
          </div>
         </div>
        </section>

                 <div class="preview-text spaced spaced-top story-preview spaced-md hddn-mble hddn-dktp hddn-tbl hddn-mble">
                  The prospect of a takeover of The Hartford Financial Services Group -- the last major insurer headquartered in Hartford, with a long, storied history -- piled on another worry for the city of Hartford.

Ned Lamont has revised the state’s vaccination timeline, moving up to April 5 the date all residents 16 and older will be eligible to receive shots. “I think you’re going to find by mid-May we’re going to be going out trying to convince people that they ought to come in and get vaccinated,” the governor said, predicting by that point most of those seeking vaccines will have been able to schedule appointments.
